I remember watching a YouTube video a while back that explains the Alien's AI in detail, breaking down everything about how it works, and I was fascinated by how intricate and thought out the Alien's AI was. If it weren't for that AI the devs designed, the game wouldn't have been the same at all.  The devs tailor programmed the AI to maximize immersion, as well as control pacing, suspense and pressure dynamically. The AI is even programmed to learn from the player's actions and adapt to the way you play and things you do (not a new concept at the time, but that on top of the tailor made AI just made the game even better).  I love Alien Isolation so much. It is my favorite horror game ever made, and definitely top five games of all time in my mind.

Great update as always. Killer suggestion: Anton Chigurh Source: No Country for Old Men Alternate skin: Judge Glanton (Blood Meridian)  Weapon: Restrained bolt Ability: Uncomfortable presence. Anton has a way of making people unnerved, just by looking at him. Anton can activate this ability while within sight of the other players. Doing so slows him down to a regular player's speed but as long as he's visible, skill checks WILL FAIL. This ability is metered and has a cooldown period that refills only when it is empty. While active, the terror radius will have an unpleasant drone that will signal to players that death awaits around every posssible corner.  Perks focusing on creating division between players No good deed: Healing another player causes them to be revealed. Keeping your word: Performing a mori causes the last player who had a co-op action with the victim to be wounded and revealed. Padded footsteps: Transfer your terror radius to the least damaged target provided that all others have been wounded once, confusing the players.  Items:  Bloody handcuffs: Ambushing a player while using padded footsteps allows the player to activate a QTE. Successfully doing so results in instantly downing the victim. Other victims can try breaking the hold using flashlights and firecrackers  and the victim can break free using pallets if reachable.  Special quarter. Activating any of the perks above builds up a token up to 6 levels. The item can be called once a survivor is downed with a 50-50 chance of right call. A success can inflict a deep wound on the nearest active player whereas a failure revives the downed player. Each level adds an additional 5% chance of succeess for a maximum of 75%. A single call consumes all levels, so it's always an act of opportunity management. Memento Mori: Anton blasts out the knees of a player with his silenced shotgun as they crawl away, he finishes them with the restraining bolt to the head.

New Killer - The Xenomorph  Killer Power  Hidden Pursuit  A series of tunnels become available on the map when the Xenomorph is in play. By accessing a Control Station, it can enter these tunnels to quickly move around the map, detect the presence of nearby Survivors, and speed up the cooldown time of its Runner Mode ability. Exiting a Control Station tags nearby Survivors with Killer Instinct.  Special Ability: Runner Mode  The Xenomorph enters Runner Mode automatically when not on cooldown. In Runner Mode, the Xenomorph walks on four legs and becomes stealthier, reducing its Terror Radius. While in Runner Mode the Xenomorph also has access to a brutal Tail Attack.
